      <p>This is a <b>list of national capitals</b>, including <a href="/wiki/Capital_city" title="Capital city">capitals</a> of <a href="/wiki/Territory_(administrative_division)" class="mw-redirect" title="Territory (administrative division)">territories</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dependent_territory" title="Dependent territory">dependencies</a>, non-sovereign states including <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">associated states</a> and entities whose <a href="/wiki/Sovereignty" title="Sovereignty">sovereignty</a> is <a href="/wiki/Territorial_dispute" title="Territorial dispute">disputed</a>. </p>
      <p>The capitals included on this list are those associated with states or territories listed by the international standard <a href="/wiki/ISO_3166-1" title="ISO 3166-1">ISO 3166-1</a>, or that are included in the <a href="/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition" title="List of states with limited recognition">list of states with limited recognition</a>. </p>
      <p>Sovereign states and observer states within the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> are shown in bold text. </p>

         <td><a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(official)</span></td> 
         <td rowspan="2"><b><span class="flagicon" style="display:inline-block;width:25px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600"></span>&nbsp;<a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a></b></td> 
         <td>The Dutch constitution refers to Amsterdam as the "<a href="/wiki/Capital_of_the_Netherlands" title="Capital of the Netherlands">capital</a>". Also of the public bodies of: <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Flag_of_Bonaire.svg/23px-Flag_of_Bonaire.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Flag_of_Bonaire.svg/35px-Flag_of_Bonaire.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1e/Flag_of_Bonaire.svg/45px-Flag_of_Bonaire.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="400">&nbsp;</span>Bonaire, <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Flag_of_Saba.svg/23px-Flag_of_Saba.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Flag_of_Saba.svg/35px-Flag_of_Saba.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Flag_of_Saba.svg/45px-Flag_of_Saba.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span>Saba and <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Flag_of_Sint_Eustatius.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sint_Eustatius.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Flag_of_Sint_Eustatius.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sint_Eustatius.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Flag_of_Sint_Eustatius.svg/45px-Flag_of_Sint_Eustatius.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span>Sint Eustatius. </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/The_Hague" title="The Hague">The Hague</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(de facto)</span></td> 
         <td>The Dutch government is located in The Hague, which also hosts the <a href="/wiki/Noordeinde_Palace" title="Noordeinde Palace">monarch</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_of_the_Netherlands" title="Cabinet of the Netherlands">government ministries</a>, <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_Netherlands" title="Supreme Court of the Netherlands">judiciary</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_in_the_Netherlands" title="List of diplomatic missions in the Netherlands">diplomatic missions</a>. </td>

         <td><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/Laayoune" title="Laayoune">El Aaiún</a></span> <span style="font-size:85%;">(declared)</span></td> 
         <td rowspan="2"><span class="flagicon" style="display:inline-block;width:25px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="300"></span>&nbsp;<a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Western Sahara</a>&nbsp;<sup class="reference" id="ref_cnone"><a href="#endnote_cnone">[c]</a></sup></td> 
         <td rowspan="2">The Sahrawi Republic, recognised by <a href="/wiki/Legal_status_of_Western_Sahara#States_recognizing_the_SADR" class="mw-redirect" title="Legal status of Western Sahara">82 states</a>, claims the mostly <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Moroccan</a> controlled <a href="/wiki/Western_Sahara" title="Western Sahara">Western Sahara</a>. Moroccan controlled territory includes El Aaiún, and Morocco claims all <a href="/wiki/Free_Zone_(region)" title="Free Zone (region)">Sahrawi controlled territory</a>. <a href="/wiki/Tifariti" title="Tifariti">Tifariti</a> is now the <a href="/wiki/Temporary_capital" title="Temporary capital">temporary capital</a> (instead of <a href="/wiki/Bir_Lehlou" title="Bir Lehlou">Bir Lehlou</a> earlier) of the SADR. Some government and military structures reside in exile in <a href="/wiki/Tindouf" title="Tindouf">Tindouf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> See <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Politics of the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Politics of the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>. </td>
        </tr>

        <tr> 
         <td rowspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(disputed)</span></td> 
         <td><b><span class="flagicon" style="display:inline-block;width:25px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/21px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/32px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/41px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1100" data-file-height="800"></span>&nbsp;<a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a></b> <span style="font-size:85%;">(de facto)</span></td> 
         <td rowspan="2">The <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem_Law" title="Jerusalem Law">Jerusalem Law</a> states that "Jerusalem, complete and united, is the capital of Israel" and the city serves as the seat of the Israeli government and its institutions. <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_478" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 478">United Nations Security Council Resolution 478</a> declared the Jerusalem Law "null and void" and called on member states to withdraw their diplomatic missions from Jerusalem. Most countries currently maintain their embassies in and around <a href="/wiki/Tel_Aviv" title="Tel Aviv">Tel Aviv</a>. The <a href="/wiki/United_States_recognition_of_Jerusalem_as_capital_of_Israel" title="United States recognition of Jerusalem as capital of Israel">United States recognized Jerusalem as the capital</a> and moved <a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_the_United_States,_Jerusalem" title="Embassy of the United States, Jerusalem">its embassy</a> there in May 2018. <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> Many countries officially adhere to the proposal that Jerusalem have international status, as called for in the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Partition_Plan_for_Palestine" title="United Nations Partition Plan for Palestine">1947 Partition Plan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">State of Palestine</a>, a <i><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">de jure</a></i> state, claims <a href="/wiki/East_Jerusalem" title="East Jerusalem">East Jerusalem</a> as its capital. See <a href="/wiki/Status_of_Jerusalem" title="Status of Jerusalem">Status of Jerusalem</a> and <a href="/wiki/Positions_on_Jerusalem" class="mw-redirect" title="Positions on Jerusalem">Positions on Jerusalem</a>. </td>
        </tr>

         <td><a href="/wiki/Taipei" title="Taipei">Taipei</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(de facto)</span></td> 
         <td><span class="flagicon" style="display:inline-block;width:25px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600"></span>&nbsp;<a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a></td> 
         <td>Officially the Republic of China (ROC), it has been competing for recognition with the <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People's Republic of China</a> (PRC) as the sole Chinese government since 1949. Taiwan controls the island of Taiwan and its associated islands, Quemoy, Matsu, the Pratas, and part of the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Spratly_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Spratly-9">[Note 1]</a></sup> The territory of Taiwan is claimed in whole by the People's Republic of China.<sup id="cite_ref-TAI2_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TAI2-10">[Note 2]</a></sup> The Republic of China participates in the <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> and a number of non-UN international organizations such as the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Organization" title="World Trade Organization">World Trade Organization</a>, <a href="/wiki/International_Olympic_Committee" title="International Olympic Committee">International Olympic Committee</a> and others under a variety of pseudonyms, most commonly <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Taipei" title="Chinese Taipei">Chinese Taipei</a>. </td>
        </tr>

         <td><a href="/wiki/States_and_territories_of_Australia" title="States and territories of Australia">External territory</a> of <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/Willemstad" title="Willemstad">Willemstad</a></td>

         <td>Self-governing country within the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Kingdom of the Netherlands</a>. </td>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_national_capitals&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;"> 
       <div class="mw-references-wrap">
        <ol class="references"> 
         <li id="cite_note-Spratly-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Spratly_9-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The sovereignty over the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a> is disputed by the PRC, the ROC, <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> (part), <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> (part), and <a href="/wiki/Brunei" title="Brunei">Brunei</a> (part). Except Brunei, each of these countries occupies part of the islands (see <a href="/wiki/List_of_territorial_disputes" title="List of territorial disputes">List of territorial disputes</a>).</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-TAI2-10"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-TAI2_10-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In 1949, the Republic of China government led by the <a href="/wiki/Kuomintang" title="Kuomintang">Kuomintang</a> (KMT) lost the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Civil_War" title="Chinese Civil War">Chinese Civil War</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Communist Party of China">Communist Party of China</a> (CPC) and set up a provisional capital in Taipei. The CPC established the People's Republic. As such, the <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_Taiwan" title="Political status of Taiwan">political status</a> of the ROC and the <a href="/wiki/Legal_status_of_Taiwan" class="mw-redirect" title="Legal status of Taiwan">legal status of Taiwan</a> (alongside the <a href="/wiki/Free_Area_of_the_Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Free Area of the Republic of China">territories</a> under ROC jurisdiction) are in dispute. In 1971, the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> gave the <a href="/wiki/China_and_the_United_Nations" title="China and the United Nations">China seat</a> to the PRC instead of the ROC: most states recognize the PRC to be the <a href="/wiki/One-China_policy" title="One-China policy">sole legitimate representative of all China</a>, and the UN classifies Taiwan as "<a href="/wiki/Taiwan_Province,_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Taiwan Province, People's Republic of China">Taiwan, Province of China</a>". The ROC has <i>de facto</i> relations with most sovereign states. A significant political movement within Taiwan advocates <a href="/wiki/Taiwan_independence" class="mw-redirect" title="Taiwan independence">Taiwan independence</a>.</span> </li> 
        </ol>
       </div>
      </div>
